Sports News

World Games Weightlifting Rules – Translation and Publication by the China National Amateur Athletic Federation for Training and Reference of Domestic Martial Arts Practitioners 204

Our country's weightlifting (stone lock and stone dumbbell), and the weightlifting competition specified in the World Games program are largely the same in method, but their application of movements and competition rules have special regulations. Only through legal training and considerable experience can one compete in strength. The National Amateur Athletic Federation has specially translated and published the general rules of weightlifting competition and training rules in the World Games, for the training and reference of domestic martial arts practitioners. The rules are as follows (these English rules have been reviewed and approved by the International Weightlifting Federation and reviewed, approved, and adopted by the China National Amateur Athletic Federation):

(1) Lifting Rules

First Type: Two-Handed Press

First Movement: Place the bar horizontally in front of you, grasp it with both hands, and with a simple and clear movement, take one leg into a half-lunge or a bent-leg bouncing stance, lifting the bar to shoulder height, then pause with the bar resting on the chest or close to the upper arms. Move both feet closer on a straight line to a distance of no more than 40 centimeters.

Second Movement: After completing the first movement, hold still for two seconds, then use both arms simultaneously to slowly lift the bar upwards (without using quick movements to gain momentum) until both arms are fully extended. Hold still in this position for two seconds. During this upward movement, the athlete's head and body should remain on a vertical line at all times. (Important Point) After completing the first movement, the bar must touch the chest. After touching, do not start the upward movement before the referee signals (a pat is the signal). If the athlete cannot hold the bar on the chest, they should notify the referee before the competition. The basis for these athletes' initial upward movement should be at the point where the collarbone and sternum connect.

Illegal Movements: During the upward movement, if the athlete's head and body are not on a vertical line, the heels are raised, or the legs show a slight bend, these are all illegal movements.

Second Type: Two-Handed Snatch

Place the bar horizontally in front of you, grasp it with both hands, and with a simple and clear movement, snatch it up from the ground, lifting it over the head until both arms are vertically extended. Taking one leg into a half-lunge or a bent-leg bouncing stance is acceptable. The bar rises along the body, the movement is continuous and uninterrupted, and no part of the body other than the feet may touch the ground.

After lifting the bar, hold still for two seconds. The arms and legs must remain in their original position. The feet should stand on a straight line no more than 40 centimeters apart.

When performing this movement, the hands should extend directly from the shoulders, be on the same plane as the shoulders, and not move left or right. (Important Point) A single movement is the basic principle of this exercise. Do not delay the movement before the wrist rotates. The wrist should rotate after the bar passes overhead.

Third Type: Two-Handed Clean and Jerk

Place the bar horizontally in front, grasp it with both hands, and with a simple and clear movement, take one leg into a half-lunge or a bent-leg bouncing stance, lifting the bar to shoulder height. The bar should rest on the chest or close to the upper arms. The bar must not touch the chest before reaching shoulder height. After this, move both feet along a straight line, bend both legs, and with a sudden movement, straighten the legs and arms, pushing the bar up into a vertically extended position. In this final position, hold still for two seconds. The feet should be on a straight line, no more than 40 centimeters apart. The upward movement must not be re-tried.

(Illegal Movements) Using the knees to support the ground, or the bar touching any part of the body before reaching shoulder height, are illegal movements.

(2) General Competition Rules

(A) Whether pressing, snatching, or clean and jerking, there are no special restrictions on the leg movements when thrusting the chest or bouncing up. (B) When gripping the bar, it is absolutely forbidden to cover the last segment of the thumb with all four fingers together to gain an advantage. (C) If the results of the lifted weight are equal, the athlete with the lighter body weight wins the competition.

(3) Trial Lift Rules

(A) Each athlete has three attempts for each type of lift (not for each weight). (B) Each time the weight is increased, it must not be less than five kilograms. However, on the third attempt, they may be allowed to increase it by 2.5 kilograms. An increase of 2.5 kilograms indicates that it is their final attempt. (C) Each time the weight is attempted, it can be increased, but not reduced compared to the previous one. (If the first attempt is successful, the second attempt should be increased. If the first attempt is unsuccessful, the second attempt should be with the original weight, not reduced.) (D) All types of trial lifts should be held within a square area of four meters. (E) Each weight class of athletes can determine their own minimum weight, which the competition management prepares and places in the arena in advance. (F) Once the weight has been attempted, it must not be reduced. (G) Attempts held inside the trial lift area are considered official attempts. (H) If an attempt fails, the referee should grant a three-minute rest period before the second attempt. Before completing all types of attempts, the bar must not be taken out of the arena, except for increasing the weight. (I) Even if the movements are not perfectly aligned, but there is a clear tendency to lift, the referee may judge it as one attempt. Lifting the bar to knee height is also counted as one attempt.

(4) Heavy Bar Structure

The heavy bar consists of a steel round shaft with metal discs attached to each end (the total weight of the bar is adjusted by adding or removing discs). The gap between the shaft and the ground for heavy bars used in international competitions is at most 21.1 centimeters, and the diameter of the largest disc must not exceed 45 centimeters. The diameter of the shaft is 2.8 kilograms.

(5) Weight Classes

The weighing of each athlete's body weight is held before the competition, divided into five classes according to the following standards: Light, Junior Lightweight, Middleweight, Junior Heavyweight, and Heavyweight.

Lightweight: Body weight 60 kilograms (132.2 pounds) and below

Junior Lightweight: Body weight 67.5 kilograms (148.5 pounds) and below

Middleweight: Body weight 75 kilograms (165 pounds) and below

Junior Heavyweight: Body weight 82.5 kilograms (181.5 pounds) and below

Heavyweight: Body weight 8.5 kilograms (181.5 pounds) and above

(6) Penalties

Athletes with improper behavior or loud disputes should receive one warning. If they receive two warnings, they will be disqualified from the competition. If disrespectful or insulting behavior is discovered, they may be immediately disqualified without warning.

Attached is a table of results for the winners of each class in the 1932 International Weightlifting Competition

Ministry of Education Order: Submit Reports on Nursing Vocational Schools 211

(Nanjing, 19th) The Ministry of Education ordered all departments to state that nursing education is a type of vocational education facility. The Ministry previously decided to follow the regulations for vocational schools and established temporary regulations for senior nursing vocational schools, ordering compliance. However, many of the vocational school survey forms reported by the provinces and cities did not include this type of school, and many privately established schools were not registered according to regulations. Therefore, all public and private hospitals in the provinces and cities that have nursing schools, training classes, or training institutes, totaling more than 160, should quickly investigate and clarify the situation within their jurisdiction and complete registration by the end of this month. Those that do not meet the senior level should also fill out the forms and submit them for approval. In addition to following the regulations for private schools and filling out various forms, they should also report a summary of the teaching hospitals for evaluation. Furthermore, if there are already public senior nursing vocational schools or nursing departments affiliated with schools in the provinces and cities, they should be identified and reported to the Ministry for reference within two weeks of receiving this document. Compliance and reporting are required.

City Education Bureau Issues List of Self-Study Books for Summer School Students; Submission of Notes Required on Schedule; Reading to Commence Immediately 212

The Shanghai City Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to all municipal and registered private primary schools in the city, stating: "Regarding the regulations for the Education Bureau's summer school for primary school teachers and staff, they have been revised and promulgated. As Article 4 of these regulations stipulates that 'students should engage in self-study before enrollment, based on a reading list of books for various subjects provided by the Bureau; each student should select and read books from the designated list for each subject, and create notes to be submitted for review upon the opening of summer school,' the Bureau hereby issues a list of self-study books for students of this year's summer school. All students who are to enroll from each school must strictly adhere to the regulations, carefully assess their own academic abilities, and commence purchasing and reading books immediately. Each subject should involve reading at least 80,000 characters, and notes must be submitted on schedule. However, as the list of books for each subject offered this year may not fully suit the level of all students, permission is granted for students to select and read other similar books with approval, in addition to the designated list. Notes, however, must still be submitted uniformly. No excuses or delays should be made. As this concerns the self-improvement of students, all school teachers and staff should diligently comply. The principals of each school bear the responsibility for leadership and supervision, and should especially lead by example and diligently carry out these duties. Further regulations regarding the registration procedures and the establishment of addresses for the summer school, as well as admission tickets, will be announced later. For now, a list of self-study books for students of this year's summer school is issued for compliance. Do not neglect this order." Zhang You San Speaks on How to Study Education 213

Yesterday marked the tenth day of the National Reading Movement Conference, organized by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association. The association specially invited Professor Zhang You San of Jinan University to broadcast a lecture on "How to Study Education" on the Sino-Western Radio Station. The full transcript of Zhang You San's lecture is as follows:

First Determine the Standpoint: The invitation from the Cultural Construction Association asks about how to study education. First, it is necessary to determine from what standpoint to study, and then we can talk about how to study. Because education is a subject that everyone should care about. Education is a process in society that carries on the past and opens up the future. Everyone in society should study education. Those who are fathers and brothers in the family have the responsibility to educate their children and should also learn a little about the principles of education. If we are willing to engage in education, then we must study education. However, those engaged in education can also be divided into two categories. One category is ordinary teachers. Their study of education only needs to be a general understanding. The other category is education experts. They take the study of various issues in education as a lifelong career. Their research needs to be more in-depth. What I am talking about today is mainly for the research of experts. Others can also use it as a reference.

Scientific Research: There are three ways to study education. The first is the recognition of facts. This type of research can be called scientific research. Their research attitude is exactly the same as that of natural sciences. Their purpose is to collect all kinds of facts related to education to provide a factual basis for education. The facts to be collected in education can be roughly divided into three categories. One category belongs to the psychological, which is to seek a correct understanding of the individual's nature and its changes. The second category belongs to the social, which is to seek a correct understanding of the actual situation and needs of the society. The third category belongs to education itself, which is to seek a correct understanding of the implementation of education and its impact and results. There are many inventions in education about the methods of collecting facts. I can briefly give a few examples. One is the observation method. The difference between scientific observation and ordinary observation is that the former is more precise. How can it be precise? That is to determine the scope of the observation object and only focus on observing one thing at a time, and record what is observed at any time, so naturally it can be precise. The three categories of facts mentioned earlier can all use the observation method. The observation method has evolved into a tracking method. This is also a kind of observation, but the effect of education is often not visible in the present, but must be expressed after many years. For example, using an educational method to educate gifted children, whether this method is suitable for the cultivation of genius must wait until these genius children have grown up to be expressed. Therefore, we must patiently track for several years to see the results. The second is the consultation method, which is to prepare a consultation form (also known as a questionnaire) or send it to the person being consulted and ask them to fill it out, or record the questions face-to-face. This method is suitable for investigating the implementation of education and soliciting the opinions of experts. However, when compiling the consultation form, the scope and nature of the questions need to be written clearly, and it should be easy for the person being consulted to fill it out. The third is the analysis method. For example, business analysis is to analyze a certain special business in life into the most detailed activities, so as to help individuals choose a career or prepare for personal life. The analysis method also includes a diagnostic method. This is an analysis specifically used to discover the individual difficulties of students in order to apply remedies. The fourth is the statistical method. General facts are often messy. If they are not sorted out, they will not show any meaning. After statistics, you can see the distribution situation, understand the central tendency and the dispersion tendency, and thus determine the reliability of the material. There is a method in statistics called counting method, which is to seriously count the number of times a certain type of fact is discovered and see how many times it is to determine the level of its importance. For example, to investigate primary school students writing wrong characters, which characters are the easiest to write wrong, it is best to check one by one from the primary school students' composition books and other works, and calculate the number to get an objective answer. The fifth is the verification method. This method can be divided into two types. A is the testing method, which is most suitable for measuring the characteristics of personality and the personality differences between people. B is the experimental method, which is to try a problem that you want to solve in the field, and then see the effect. The scientific research methods mentioned above require specialized research and must have received scientific training, have an objective attitude, meticulous analysis, and need to have a foundation in statistical knowledge. Not only must they have received considerable training when doing their own research, but also if they have not been trained, even articles written by others with discussions or reports, some of the terms in them are not easy to understand.

Philosophical Research: The second method of studying education is the establishment of educational ideals. This method can be called philosophical research. Education should indeed be based on facts, but it should not be bound by facts. Education not only maintains the existing culture, but also improves the old culture and creates a new culture. It should have an ideal for the future society and the future individual. How is this ideal established? Of course, it is necessary for people with a solid foundation and a broad vision to be able to set a valuable ideal. This kind of research cannot only be learned from education itself, but must have an understanding of various academic issues, especially economics, politics and other academic disciplines. After having a very deep research, and then using a comprehensive perspective, can we set the goal of education. This can be called the method of synthesis. Secondly, we must know that history is continuous, and all social systems have their past origins. If we do not understand the past, we cannot understand the trend of evolution. Therefore, to study education, we must use the historical method. The third is the comparative method, that is, the systems and theories of various countries, etc., that can be used for my reference should be studied. Then, we can determine the educational ideals needed at this time and place. The philosophical method includes synthesis, history, and comparison as one method. Before studying education in this way, we should first put in some effort in social science. Because education is science, it needs precise analysis. Because education is philosophy, it needs broad synthesis. People who study education need to be both precise and broad. American-style education focuses on scientific research, and European-style education focuses on philosophical research. In fact, both are important and cannot be neglected. However, researchers may as well consider the similarity of their personality and focus on one aspect.

Practical Research: As for the third type of research, it can be called practical research. Its role is to start from the facts and return to the ideal, how to cross the middle, and what steps are required. This part of education belongs to the department of methodology. The methodology I am referring to here is broad, and can include education, administration, school organization, management, selection of teaching materials, teaching methods, and so on. Although there are many theories to explore these issues, they should be thoroughly sought from practice.

Finance: Call Loan Rate Still at One Percent 214

Yesterday was Easter, and foreign firms and banks were uniformly closed for three days. However, the majority of Chinese firms operated as usual. The Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Commercial Bank of China also remained closed as in the past. The closing was stable. Spot prices rose 15 points, and futures prices rose 10 to 12 points. British cotton spot prices fell 6 points, and futures prices fell 8 to 10 points. Indian cotton was weak due to a lack of buyers and long positions closing out. Pingguoer fell 1.25 rupees, Aomula fell 3 to 3.25 rupees, and Bailuoxi fell 0.75 to 2.5 rupees. Grains: Deferred Flour Market Retraces 220

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, each month showed a flat initial trend, followed by a continuous rise, and then flattening again. With foreign wheat prices, both Chicago and Canada were slightly down by 0.08 to 0.10 yuan. When the prices opened, this month opened flat. Then, due to the current tight supply of actual flour, some small factories and outside speculators, seeing that the spring rains had been too long and fearing problems, rushed to hedge their positions. Most clients were long and did not want to sell, so the asking price steadily rose, reaching a high of 0.09 yuan. Deferred months also continued to rise by about 0.01 yuan due to smooth purchases by inland buyers. When the market opened in the afternoon, this month's prices were still very stable due to higher spot prices. Deferred months, however, were heavily sold by factories, and the weather turned sunny and milder, so from July onwards, prices uniformly retracted. Looking at the future, if the weather does not change, a bearish trend is expected. As a result, this month was still up by 0.015 yuan, May and June were unchanged, July fell by 0.01 yuan, and August and September each fell by 0.0125 yuan—sales sentiment was triggered for deferred months.

Wheat Deliveries Rare and Expensive This Month - Sales Sentiment Triggered for Deferred Months 221

Yesterday's wheat market showed a generally quiet trend after opening in the morning. With foreign wheat prices, both Chicago and Canada were only slightly down by 0.08 to 0.10 yuan. During the slack period, near-term and far-term trading was still active, and prices rotated with little gains or losses. Although there were reports of flooding in various provinces, it was not expected to cause problems with the wheat harvest, so sentiment was still peaceful. When the market opened in the afternoon, the weather was clear and sunny, and deferred flour had also retreated, so selling sentiment became smooth and sentiment turned negative. This month, due to the scarcity of deliveries, was still seeing high prices. As a result, this month rose by 0.04 yuan, July fell by 0.04 yuan, August fell by 0.06 yuan, and September fell by 0.06 yuan. The spot wheat market was still stable. Shandong Bengbu wheat opened at 4 yuan, and Hebei Ping wheat at 3.99 yuan, totaling 4,000 bags, which were purchased by Fuxin.

Oil Market: Hankou White Tung Oil Rises and Falls Again 226

White tung oil has been rising and falling repeatedly in the past month, with a wide range of fluctuations. It soars when it rises and plummets when it falls. Within a week, it rises and falls, and the price per dan fluctuates constantly by 5 to 6 yuan. Therefore, those engaged in this business find it difficult to cope with. Just two weeks ago, foreign firms in Hankou actually reached 41 yuan, but by the previous week, they had plummeted to 33 to 34 yuan. Last week, they added to 39 yuan. This week, they have seen a sharp fall again. According to a telegram received from Hankou yesterday, it has fallen to 36.2 yuan, and the situation is still difficult to establish a foothold. It is feared that 35 yuan is imminent. It is said that the reason is that the source from Changde is surging, and although the various foreign firms in Hankou are still interested in purchasing, they also want to lower the price, so Hankou firms are making transactions for Xiang tung at 21 taels of light money, revealing the fatigue of the market. However, in this era of booming export trade, it is often the case that a sharp rise follows a severe fall. This has been proven in the past, and it is generally believed that the price of 34 to 35 yuan, even if there is no possibility of a turnaround, also has a foothold. Therefore, in the current market, although it is said to be extremely tired, there is also a limit to how much further it can fall, because European and American countries still need goods, and it is common to purchase in large quantities during periods of fatigue. This is unpredictable. Although the business of foreign firms in the local area has seen some development in recent years, it is not as continuous as the source in Hankou, so transactions are sometimes available and sometimes not.

Power cloth had very wide sales and unusually high prices last year, and the distributors earned large profits. This year, imports of Power cloth flooded the market, and transactions have already been made in various places. The market price has indeed fallen sharply. Ordinary brands of solid-colored Power cloth are only selling for 3.6 yuan per yard, and patterned goods are 4.3 to 4.4 yuan, which is obviously due to too many orders being placed.

Silk and Tea: New Sui'an Green Tea Has Opened 229

Sui'an green tea in Zhejiang Province has always been the earliest to come out. This year, due to the cold weather, the tea buds are developing slowly. The tea farmers only started picking the tea the day before yesterday. Yesterday, a telegram came from that place saying that new first-batch green tea had been launched. Calculated according to the city scale, the market price opened at 60 yuan. Currently, tea merchants from all over are eager to get new tea, and demand is high. Also, because the weather is cold and deliveries are not active, the market is expected to go higher.

New Voices from the Anhui-Jiangxi Tea Market 230

After Grain Rain and approaching the Start of Summer, the tea market, traditionally a major export commodity, is once again entering its active season. Red and green tea merchants in Anhui and Jiangxi are busy strategizing and preparing to enter the market. A tense atmosphere surrounds the tea market in various production areas. Mountain dwellers who rely on tea for their livelihoods are eagerly awaiting the arrival of the "Tea God" to rescue them from poverty. However, with the overseas market experiencing a downturn, it is difficult to predict whether this year's tea market will be prosperous or bleak. The reporter will now provide an account of the recent tea industry activities in various production areas:

She County green tea is traditionally divided into foreign and domestic operations. Last year, those engaged in foreign operations suffered losses due to sluggish sales and price drops, regardless of the quality of their goods. Even though the first batch yielded a small profit, the overall result was still a deficit. Domestic tea operations focusing on scented tea suffered as routes to various provinces outside the customs were blocked, and the influx of Japanese tea into Shandong led to a decline in business. This year, foreign tea merchants, seeing no improvement in the overseas tea market, are only preparing to open about 40% of the operations compared to last year, with the rest adopting a wait-and-see approach. However, in the Choumu Cen and Wenzheng Mountain areas, some scented tea operations are still preparing to enter the market, and merchants from Hebei and Shandong are also bringing funds to the mountains to establish businesses and purchase tea. Although the market is more active than the foreign operations, it is only about 60% of what it was in previous years and cannot be considered bustling.

Tunxi is the center of the tea market in Huizhou. Since 1925, merchants have suffered repeated losses, with only a few years of small profits. In the end, they still lost more than they gained. Most of the dozens of tea merchants in the city are exhausted and lack the funds to sustain themselves. This year, only about twenty merchants have confirmed their plans to operate, while the rest are hoping for assistance from the warehouse operators and the financial sector to resume business. The decline in market activity is unprecedented. In the past, wealthy tea firms would lend money to tea vendors after Pure Brightness to cover the cost of tea picking and rice for food. Now, they are closing their doors and refusing to lend, leaving them helpless. Mountain dwellers, unable to secure loans from tea merchants, lack the resources to purchase rice, fertilizer, hire labor, and repair equipment. The stagnant atmosphere among warehouse operators, merchants, and mountain dwellers has left the Tunxi tea market without any signs of life.

Qimen black tea has suffered repeated setbacks, and tea merchants are impoverished due to heavy losses. However, as the economic lifeline of the county largely depends on tea, those tea firms that can muster the strength are struggling to resume business, hoping for some late-season gains. Currently, the new tea in the county is benefiting from the recent warm and rainy weather, and the tea buds are sprouting. White hair Mao Feng tea is ready for picking. Warehouse operators and tea merchants believe that the mountain prices may decrease this year, transportation is convenient, and tea inventories are low, so they are turning their pessimism into optimism. Various warehouses in Qimen have already started releasing funds, and the credit situation is more active than before. In addition, the Agricultural Bank of the Four Provinces is directly lending money to tea merchants. Although the financial situation is not as flexible as in previous years, it is still better than nothing. With this assistance, the tea firms are not exactly reviving, but it is estimated that about 180 tea firms in the county have resumed operations as of this ten-day period, a decrease of about 100 compared to last year.

Wuyuan green tea has excellent quality and taste and could command a high price due to its scarcity. However, the foreign merchants' appetite is weak. Although there are precious varieties, it is difficult to force them to purchase. Many of last year's high-quality eyebrow teas are still stored in Shanghai, unsold. The inventory of Shi Xiuxiu eyebrow tea is particularly large. The tea merchants have suffered losses and are unable to settle their accounts. The depth of their pain is beyond words. This year's new tea in various villages will be ready for picking at the end of the month. Fewer Shanghai warehouses are stationed in Wuyuan to release funds this year, with only Yong Shenchang no longer present. The rest are also adopting a wait-and-see approach. The tea market is relatively active only in the Beiyuan, Yanchuan, Wangcun, and Xichong areas, where preparations for operations, such as purchasing boxes, boards, firewood, and charcoal, are underway. Elsewhere, there is little news. In general, mountain dwellers lack the funds to hire labor to pick tea due to the lack of tea money released by the tea merchants and the high price of rice due to crop failures. Their predicament is difficult to describe.

In addition, Yushan green tea has the advantage of convenient transportation via the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, and the banditry in the production area has been suppressed. It is said that several tea firms are planning to open operations, so the tea market is not without hope. In Dexing, the tea-producing areas have been disrupted by bandits for many years, and farmers have migrated to other regions. The tea trees are barren, and the local economy cannot be restored in a short period of time. Households with some assets currently have no intention of engaging in the tea industry.

Spring and Autumn Magazine Special Travel Edition

Touring the City Center 231

— (Xu Haowu)

After a long spell of cold and gloomy weather, a sunny day joyfully carried me to the heart of Shanghai on a public bus.

The palatial and spacious Municipal Government building. The brightly colored Party flags fluttered atop the towering flagpoles in the gentle breeze.

Tourists, taking advantage of their leisure time, strolled up the stone steps in front of the building, admiring the Party emblem in the middle. Shedding their heavy winter clothes, their steps were light and nimble.

Clusters of pedicabs. Young men, intentionally skilled at riding, wore thin shirts and shorts, heads down, exerting their strength, the wheels whizzing across the wide surrounding roads.

The concession lived up to its name; it has dense markets and towering skyscrapers - international conspiracy, urban crime!

Stepping into the city center designed by our own people: exquisite new villages, smooth roads, lush green fields: neat and clean, full of the vitality of nature!

The city center nurtured by Shanghai, threatened by gunfire before its birth and battered by wind and rain after, should be gasping for breath. But, young as it is, it has the spirit of the Western nations. It wants to fight, it wants to compete. It wants a rational organization, perfect facilities, and an orderly cityscape. It wants to quickly, diligently, and actively bloom into a bright and splendid flower for Shanghai, to inspire the people and correct their perceptions.

Lamenting the Past at Hongyang Cave 232

— Mustard Seed

About forty li northwest of Guihua City—now the capital of Suiyuan Province—is the foot of the Daqing Mountains, which are a branch of the Yin Mountains. The mountain only has a stone cave, which the locals call "Hongyang Cave." It is said to be the place where Jiao Zan and Meng Liang, generals of the Yang family, stole bones. It is said that: "The Song general Yang Jiye was trapped by Liao soldiers, and committed suicide rather than surrender. The Liao people hid Yang's body in Hongyang Cave. Generals Jiao Zan and Meng Liang stole the bones from eight caves and died in the cave. This is that place." The cave entrance is narrow but wide inside, winding and twisting, dark and bottomless. Some people have ventured deep into the cave with torches, ascending and descending along the walls. After walking for about ten miles, they gradually heard the sound of rushing springs, sounding like angry waves. The cold wind was biting, and they could not go any further, so they had to turn back midway. More than half a li west of the cave, there is a large tomb, which the locals identify as the tomb of Jiao Zan. The tomb base is very large, rising like a small hill, with several stone horses lying on the ground. The withered grass and setting sun create a desolate scene. Although the story comes from fiction, stroking the broken steles and lamenting the predecessors can evoke many emotions. To the south of Guihua City, there is also the well-known tomb of Han Zhaojun—Qingzhong—whose loyal soul and bones will forever be remembered. Even now, it still bears traces of resisting the enemy and making peace, adding much color to this ancient capital of the southern desert.

Boating on Xuanwu Lake 233

— Yu Lilin

The Spring God staggers down, and the earth puts on a dazzling coat. Red flowers, green trees, green mountains, and green water decorate the vast space. A heart that has been suffocated for a long time is filled with active spirit. Unwilling to waste the beautiful scenery and good times, I went with Luo Ben... to Xuanwu Lake for a stroll.

After leaving Xuanwu Gate, the swaying willows by the lake flirtatiously fluttered in the wind and waves. The vast white lake was filled with many boats, weaving back and forth. Overhead was a clear blue sky. Compared to the bureaucratically heavy Nanjing city, it felt like entering another secluded world. Hundreds of tourists and boat girls gathered by the lake, the clamorous sound waves vibrating violently in the space. The cars and horses on the road were like ants, carrying many tourists, speeding towards Wuzhou Park, indicating that the spring is bright and people are enjoying themselves in time!

We also hired a boat and served as boatmen ourselves, slowly rowing to the center of the lake. The water was clear, and the breeze seemed to be kissing the lake, rippling into fluctuating blue waves. The boat was really like a lotus leaf, gently floating on the surface of the lake. Nestled in the arms of nature. Wuzhou Park was quietly silent, allowing people to appreciate its artificially cultivated art. By the lake, several clumps of bamboo made the spring scenery pleasant. The grotesque city walls were like a winding serpent, crouching by the lake. In the distance, the towering mountains were arranged in a staggered array. Jiming Temple was like a palace standing tall on the horizon. The five continents were like five chess pieces, placed on the lake. The warm sunshine bathed the universe, giving people unlimited possibilities for existence. We boated all over the lake, giving me a deep understanding of Xuanwu Lake.

As night gradually fell, we leisurely embarked on our return journey.

Snapshots along the Zhengtai Railway 234

— Dingming

The benefits of transportation development are infinite. Switzerland, because both water and land transportation are very convenient, although located between Germany, Austria, Italy, and France, in the Alps, there are millions of tourists who visit every year, and the travel expenses amount to 100 million a year, making it Switzerland's main source of wealth. This is the best example; transportation barriers can often cause a nation to become numb; while convenient transportation can make a nation invigorated and full of vitality; if you say that Switzerland is driven by waterfalls, clear lakes, and beautiful valleys, all of which can attract tourists, then, in such a large China, whether mountains: there are the Five Sacred Mountains and Tiantai, Yandang, Mogan, Lushan, Huangshan, Emei, etc., or water: there are the Yellow River, Wei River, Pearl River, as well as West Lake, Tai Lake, Dongting, Poyang, etc.; can't they compete with each other?

However, because the first prerequisite is inconvenient transportation, the landscape is dimmed; especially in the inland areas with excellent scenery, the footprints of people from other provinces are only scattered.

On the morning of Children's Day, April 4th, a team of "Zhengtai Railway Snapshot Group" departed from Shanghai. The photographer Lang Jingshan temporarily invited his artist friends Zhong Shanyin, Huang Zhongchang, and Liu Xucang, four people to travel together. This is really a good trend in the lonely art world. I heard that Mr. Lang's trip was at the invitation of Mr. Zhu Jiqing, the director of the Zhengtai Railway Bureau, to specially photograph the scenery along the 243-kilometer line from Shijiazhuang to Yangqu (Taiyuan), compile and print a special album to promote transportation; in this way, the magnificent scenic spots in the northern country are not allowed to be exclusively favored by the beautiful Jiangnan.

Watching Fish at Yuquan Temple 235

— (Ji Chengxing)

When I came out of Mrs. Hu's house, I rode my bike alone to Yuquan.

As soon as I entered the temple gate, I went to watch the fish.

The fish in the pool were swimming slowly. Because the water was very clear, I could see the bottom at a glance. I could almost count the scales of the big fish. The big ones were about fifteen or sixteen catties; the small ones were also as long as an adult's finger. The colors were also very different: some were red and yellow; some were red, yellow, and black; my favorite was the fat red carp; its mouth was the most beautiful, the fullness of its lips, and the swaying of its short temples in the water. They lived in the same environment, and I could not find any traces of estrangement. Sometimes they piled up in heaps, like our human pyramid; sometimes they kissed mouth to mouth, like we do. They did not fight, had no leaders, had no acts of aggression, and would not riot over the uneven distribution of food given by the tourists! How could this situation not make us humans feel disheartened!

Stone Bell Mountain and Shoe Mountain 236

— (Old Bell)

Stone Bell Mountain is outside the East Gate of Hukou County, Jiangxi. On the top of the mountain, there are small stone blocks that make a "clang clang" sound when hit with bricks or small stones, similar to the sound of a morning bell in a temple. This is how "Stone Bell Mountain" got its name. I have repeatedly struck these stones with my cane and bricks, and the sound is clear and crisp, which is really strange.

The area on top of the mountain is not very large, but there are quite a few houses. There is a "Zhaozhong Temple" that is quite well-built, completely dedicated to the memorial tablets of generals who pacified the Hong Yang rebellion, such as Zeng Guofan. There are also many works by Peng Yulin, Hu Linyi, and others. There are also several Western-style houses, which were built when Du Xigui was the commander of the Navy. Now, a battalion of Marines is stationed there for a long time. However, the trees and flowers are not lush.

Taking a boat from Hukou directly into Poyang Lake, after traveling about twenty miles, you can see a small mountain that looks like a shoe, which is Shoe Mountain, named after its shape. The mountain is surrounded by water, and the scene will remind us of Little Lonely Mountain, but the height and area are smaller than Little Lonely Mountain. There is a Handao Nunnery on the mountain, and the idol enshrined is the Bixia Yuanjun on the Investiture of the Gods. According to a Taoist priest, this mountain was transformed from a shoe of the Bixia Yuanjun, which is really foolish and ridiculous.

There are many fruit trees and bamboos on the mountain, and wildflowers are all over the mountain, colorful and extremely beautiful. Standing on the top of the mountain, you can see the Five Elders Peak of Lushan Mountain, which is connected to the clouds, and the vast white Poyang Lake is also faintly visible.

According to the Taoist priest, Chiang Kai-shek once visited the mountain in the summer of the year before last, taking advantage of his inspection of the Yangtze and Poyang Lake defenses, and donated two hundred yuan to the nunnery.

Lushan Mountain and White Crane Spring 237

— (Xie Mingcan)

Spring, or perhaps autumn, White Crane Spring has become a must-visit place for everyone who climbs the head of Lushan Mountain: despite the isolated and elegant Aiwanting Pavilion, with the most decorative buildings and maple trees all over the mountains and valleys, each shows its own strengths around it.

White Crane Spring is located behind the left side of Lushan Temple. There is a mountain road next to it, which is slightly higher than the top of the temple. It is built of bluestone, and its length and width are each less than two feet. The water drips from the stone crevices in the mountainside and flows into the stone well. It is clear and tasteful. The bay is well-known for dissipating heat.

Here you cannot see the thin green willows along the banks of Shuilu Chau, nor can you see the sails on the Xiangjiang River; two small stalls selling snacks and a few randomly lying carved stones are the usual decorations here.

The spring is named White Crane, and its origin is unknown, but there are two folk legends: one says that when tea is boiled with this spring water, the steam condenses into the shape of a crane, which is white, hence the name White Crane; the other says that when looking down at the bottom of the well, two cranes appear in the well. During the Qing Dynasty, it would be a local product. Once, due to the carelessness of the tribute bearer, the spring water spilled on the way, and the crane disappeared. Nowadays, judged by the eyes of modern scientists, neither has its place to stand. But taking it to explain the origin of the name is not without value, you must know that the origin of many place names in our country is explained by similar legends!

White Crane Spring is so monotonous, and its taste is no more superb than the springs in the countryside, but whether it is new or old friends, once they climb Lushan Mountain, they will pay a visit. Of course, the location is adjacent to the mountain path; its alluring name may be part of the reason?

Spring Frolic in Suzhou City 238

— Yan Boguang

The huge wheel of time has turned to the season of great spring, and famous scenic spots everywhere have added many footprints of tourists. Of the springs in the south of the Yangtze River, the one that makes people most nostalgic has to be Suzhou, which is like paradise! Although West Lake in Hangzhou is also a good place for tourists to linger, it is not as good as Suzhou with its soft Wu dialect.

Before the autumn wind has been blowing for too long, there are already many women on Guanqian Street wearing tight coats. However, after spring has arrived in the world, the biting spring breeze still relentlessly invades people's muscles and bones, but the women of Suzhou have already changed into spring clothes. If we stare at them, we can see the purple marks of the wind on their jade arms, and the cold shape of their breasts trembling slightly, ah! It really fits the common saying of Suzhou people: "If you want to be charming, freeze to scream." Intoxicating spring! You rely on women to embellish it!

Tiger Hill is the most interesting place, and it is impossible not to enjoy it in Suzhou. The scenery on the mountain is worth lingering on. But when we return to the inn and climb into bed, we think of the scenery of the day: and we hear the nightingales and swallows in the next room, tossing and turning and unable to sleep. At that time, we are about to hum a song; "The colors of spring annoy people and they can't sleep, the moon moves the shadow of the flower onto the railing."

There are many scenic spots in Suzhou, such as Tianping, Lingyan, Tianchi, Huashan Qionglong, Guanyin, etc., which cannot be said all at once, and are very suitable for ordinary ladies and gentlemen to have fun in spring, to enjoy and feast on the spring colors.

Grand Reunion of Classical and Emerging 239

Evening Smoke at Linwu Mountain 240

— Wu Yafei

As the boat enters Turtle Mountain Islet, one can see a not-so-high hill; surrounded by mountains, it is the shortest bluestone mountain. There are no large trees on it, and no forests can be found. The mountain is barren and bare, standing abruptly, with rugged rocks and towering cliffs. At the foot of the mountain slope, there are two student stone caves, which are Linwu Caves, and some people call them Dragon Caves. The cave is more than a zhang high, and also a zhang wide, and about three or four zhang deep, but it is not bottomless, because it is gradually deeper and smaller, so there is no way to measure its depth. There are many steles at the entrance of the cave, many of which have been eroded, and the handwriting is also blurred and difficult to distinguish; however, the ancient characters of "Ninth Cave Heaven under Heaven" can still be faintly seen. There are many bats in the cave, and they are not afraid of people, flying all day long between the right holes. There is shallow water under the cave, and the sound of ding-dong is endless. It is said that this cave can lead to Hubei and Hunan. It is only necessary to have a full torch and a salted duck egg to illuminate Hubei and Hunan and eat Hubei and Hunan. In the depths of the cave are dragon beds, stone tables, and exotic treasures; because there were originally two jade dragons entrenched in the cave. This mountain was originally called Linwu Mountain, but because of this legend? Therefore, the villagers only know that it is called Longdong Mountain. On the mountainside facing east, there is also a "Yanggu Cave", which is high, open, and dry. However, there is a Guanyin stone statue at the entrance of the cave. The mountain produces fragrant valley swords, which are shaped like lilac grass, with a clear fragrance and sweetness. Eating too much will cause bleeding in the nostrils. After the plum rain season, a kind of stone fungus will grow on the stone slab. After picking it off and washing away the sand and mud, it can be made into a soup, and its taste is excellent.

After going ashore from Zhenxia Port, walking through a long brick street, and standing on a small bridge, you can see a row of sandy roads, winding from the field to the foot of Linwu Mountain. There is a "Wuai Nunnery" to the south of the mountain, which is said to be the place where Liu Xiangnu attained enlightenment. The incense in the nunnery is also very prosperous, but although this is a nunnery, there are no nuns in it, but only monks.

There is a flower medicine altar in the east courtyard of the nunnery, on which various wonderful flowers and plants that bloom in all seasons are planted. To the south is a row of study rooms, with bright windows and clean desks, antiques, calligraphy, and paintings, which are arranged very elegantly. Pushing open the window, you can also overlook the vast Taihu Lake and the dots of sails; especially in the early morning, watching the sunrise, which is as big as a gong, slowly rising from the horizon in the east. In summer, it is even more of a summer resort, because the climate on the mountain is at most only ninety degrees. If you are there in the evening in autumn, you will really have the feeling of "the falling glow and the lonely prosper flying together, and the autumn water sharing the same color with the long sky"!

After passing through a line of sky, we climbed up the mountain peak by grasping vines. Flat as a tabletop, wide as a reed mat, stone slabs are everywhere, and an unfinished stone tower rises up like an old man. There is also a hole on it, as big as a dou, and the depth is bottomless. The villagers burn discarded paper, and all the ashes are poured here.

Standing on a cliff and looking down, we can only see a clear stream at the foot of the mountain, running along the foot of the mountain, all the way to the rice paddies in front.

It was already dusk, and the roofs of the houses in the village were showing wisps of smoke, so the Linwu Mountain was also surrounded by mist. It is really a strange scene; we feel like we are in the depths of white clouds, misty and hazy, and all the surrounding scenery has changed into a blurred posture: "It's so beautiful! It's so great!" We couldn't help but shout like this.

Shen Bao Radio Weekly

New 6G7 Composite Vacuum Tube 241

— Li Yuanqing

— Full-Wave Rectification and Pentode Powerful Output Tube —

Because modern radios require a small and exquisite body as an important condition, it is necessary to think about the problem of reducing the number of vacuum tubes. To reduce the number of vacuum tubes, each vacuum tube must serve several functions. Past vacuum tubes, such as zA76B7 and 55, were produced in response to this need.

Recently, Canadian Radio Corporation has released a new 6G7 vacuum tube, which combines a full-wave rectifier tube and a pentode powerful output tube. It is expected that after the introduction of this vacuum tube, the general small radios will have more significant progress and amazing development! The filament voltage of the 6G7 vacuum tube is 636V. The output power of the pentode part is about I.8W. The base has seven pins. The old name of the tube was 89RS. Recently, in order to meet the standard naming of the Radio Manufactured Association of the United States, it has been renamed.

The attached diagram shows the internal structure and wiring of the 6G7 vacuum tube when in use. H is the common filament, P1 and P2 are the screen poles of the rectifier part, and k1 is the cathode of the part. Usually, the filter circuit in the B electrical appliance is probably connected to the B+ place. Here, in order to reduce the bottom foot of a vacuum tube, it is changed to the B1 end. (If it is connected to B+, the curtain grid of the pentode part cannot be directly connected to K1.) P3, G1SG, K2, etc. are all the corresponding poles of the pentode part. Their function is the same as that of ordinary pentode tubes, which readers already know well, so I will not repeat them here.

After the 6G7 vacuum tube is used together with 6A7, it becomes a wonderful three-lamp superheterodyne radio. In the past, the popular small superheterodyne radios on the market always required at least four lamps to distribute various functions. At this point, the old appearance can be changed and a new look can be given.

Various Uses of Variable Resistors 242

— Qing Shi

Regarding the various different uses of variable resistors, let me write down the twelve types I know. The one used here is best at 100,000 ohms, because this amount is the most suitable for most of the following experiments. However, in Figures 1, 4, 10, and 11, it is more appropriate to use a 10,000 ohm one.

Figure 1 - The resistor is connected in series in the antenna, or connected between the antenna and the ground wire, so that the excessive broadcasting can be

Figure 2 - The 100,000 or 200,000 ohm resistor is connected in series on the screen grid circuit of the high-frequency or intermediate-frequency amplifier tube, which allows us to use the correct voltage on the screen grid.

Figure 3 - A volume control (100,000 ohms), which is installed on the secondary side of a low-frequency transformer, is also a simple way to reduce excessive broadcasting.

Figure 4 - A method of feedback management in a detector tube, using it to weaken the feedback circuit. (10,000 ohms) The feedback coil is directly facing the secondary coil and fixed inside the machine. The increase or decrease of the feedback force is only obtained from the variable resistor.

Figure 5 - The tone quality converter is connected in series with a fixed capacitor of 0.0003 microfarads and installed on the loudspeaker. When the amount of resistance is reduced, the bass tones will be adjusted well, and the sharp hiss will also be reduced proportionally.

Figure 6 - The resistor (100,000 to 200,000 ohms) is installed on the screen grid of a detector tube, which allows the screen grid to obtain the correct and appropriate voltage.

Figure 7 - Volume control and tone quality conversion use a 100,000 to 200,000 ohm resistor, which is connected to both ends of the grid resistor of the low-frequency amplifier tube. The capacitor connected in series is 0.004 to 0.006 microfarads.

Figure 8 - Volume control connected to the loudspeaker can reduce the power without changing the tone quality. (100,000 ohms).

Figure 9 - The variable resistor (200,000 ohms) is placed in the screen grid circuit to adjust the power of the high-frequency or intermediate-frequency amplifier tube, or the detector tube. The blocking capacitor is one microfarad. (To be continued)

Another Simple Test Method for Good or Bad Magnetic Loudspeakers 243

— Yong Yan

The loudspeaker is the voice of the radio. If the loudspeaker is not good, no matter how sophisticated the structure of the radio is, the sound must not be good. Therefore, considerable attention must be paid to it when purchasing to avoid mistakenly buying inferior products. Now I will introduce a simple test method as follows:

During the test, connect a resistor in series (if the voltage is 220 volts AC, use a 10,000 ohm resistor; for 110 volts, use a 5,000 ohm resistor. This instruction is not necessarily fixed, and can be slightly increased or decreased at will.) and insert it into the socket of the household power cord. At this time, if the speaker coil is intact, an AC sound of 50 cycles (or 60 or 25 cycles) will be emitted; otherwise, there is a break in the coil. If there is miscellaneous noise in addition to the AC sound, the paper cone must be broken, or the position of the iron sheet (Armature) that vibrates to make sound is improper and should be repaired. If the emitted AC sound is harmonious and not sharp, this loudspeaker will be able to faithfully emit low-frequency sound waves. When listening to Western music, it is very harmonious and pleasant.

Pay close attention during the test to prevent electric shock. There is no danger to the loudspeaker.

Radio in Beiping 244

— Dian

There is no need to introduce Beiping to readers. It is the area with the highest culture in the whole country and the most developed education, but the latest tool for communication and culture - radio - is too backward in this ancient city. It is neither as popular as in Shanghai, nor does it have a broadcasting station as large as in Nanjing. There are now a total of four formal broadcasting stations in Beiping:

The first one is the earliest established Beiping Radio Broadcasting Station (call sign is XGOP, power is 100 watts, frequency is 952.3 kHz). It broadcasts for about eight hours a day, but almost all of it is used to broadcast theater operas, and because the machinery is outdated, obstacles often occur during broadcasting.

The second one is the British merchant Zengmao Foreign Company's (Marconolo) radio station (call sign is XOMO, power is 118 watts). It also broadcasts for about eight hours a day. This is a Western radio station. Although it has been registered with the Ministry of Transportation, the broadcasting rights still do not belong to us. In addition to broadcasting Western music records every day, it also sometimes broadcasts music from the Beidong Hotel. In addition, it broadcasts two hours of Chinese records and advertisements every day.

The third one is the newly established Hebei Broadcasting Station (call sign is PGOT, power is 500 watts, frequency is 1230 kHz). It broadcasts for ten hours a day, and the programs are better than other radio stations, and the broadcasting results are not bad. In Jiangnan, if you use a radio with better selectivity, you can also receive its broadcasts.

The fourth one is the Yuying Middle School Radio Station (call sign is XHPA, power is 30 watts, frequency is 1194 kHz). This is an amateur radio station. The broadcasting time is not fixed, and the programs only include records, music, and celebrity speeches. It is not often broadcast now.

A Good News 245

Kangmao Radio Company, located at 47 Ningbo Road in this city, has always managed famous American radios, such as Yuais, Eagle King, Feige, Aikai, etc. The company's repair department used to only repair radios of its own company. Now it is heard that the company will expand the repair department in response to the needs of all sectors of society, and purchase the latest instruments to serve all sectors of society. In order to facilitate all sectors of society, the repair department will be moved to Daqinglikou, Nanjing Road for business, which is truly good news for those who have radios.

Shen Bao This City Supplement

Tan Yan

Resolving Age-Old Feuds in the Ash of Cigars 246

— Feng

A National News Agency dispatch from Paris on the 17th stated that diplomats from France and Germany may soon be able to resolve age-old feuds over cigars and ashes at the conference table. I think that if age-old feuds can be resolved over cigars and ashes, then Chen Gongbo's ashes can really govern the country and bring peace to the world.

Although the Council of the League of Nations passed the resolutions of France, Britain, and Italy, it still could not solve the difficult problems in Europe caused by Germany's rearmament, because the paper tiger of the League of Nations had long been seen through, and the result was worthless. Now, to control Germany's rearmament and stage another performance of "Heroes' Meeting," no matter how many cigars and ashes are consumed, I am afraid that the more they consume, the more they will feel smoggy and still unable to solve the German problem.

Any organization or group, if only a few people manipulate it in the middle, will absolutely not be able to take care of the interests and well-being of all members. This is a common problem in collective organizations, and the League of Nations is no exception. Therefore, at this conference, with the first cigar ash, Soviet Foreign Commissioner Litvinov (because the Soviet representative spoke first) dropped a bomb, what is called advocating the reprimand of unilateral abandonment of treaty obligations should be applied to other continents, the same as in Europe, etc. When this bomb was dropped, even though British Foreign Minister Simon immediately asked Litvinov to withdraw his reservation, and Frenchmen Laval and Aloisi also resigned for it, although this bomb did not explode in the end, it had already frightened the committee members pale. Cigar ashes sometimes cannot only fail to resolve old feuds, but can sometimes increase old feuds, which is also unpredictable.

Moreover, before the Council of the League of Nations passed the resolutions of the three countries, Germany had issued a warning, saying that if the countries of the world adopt the resolutions of the Stresa Conference, Germany under the rule of the National Socialist Party will never return to the League of Nations, and the German government will take an independent attitude, that is, Germany has been discriminated against by other countries and must have greater military power. This warning was issued by the spokesperson of German leader Hitler, and it cannot be compared to the words of ordinary irresponsible people. Looking at it from this point of view, the ashes of cigars may not have the effect of resolving age-old feuds, but may instead add fuel to the fire and increase the retaliatory nature of age-old feuds.

In short, facts speak louder than words. Since the many cigar ashes in the past could not solve the current difficulties, how can we expect the current cigar ashes to have unexpected effects? This is something that everyone can see, and the tearing up of treaties in the past, in addition to tearing up treaties, also forcibly occupied other people's land with violence. The tearing up of treaties now is just rearming for self-defense. How can we say that a country is not allowed to build up its military and defend its territory? If we compare the two, which reason is sufficient? It can be decided without saying a word, and the League of Nations can only pretend to be deaf and dumb and not act as a matchmaker. No wonder today there are many cigar ashes in the League of Nations meeting, which are equal to the cigar ashes in a wine shop, only for temporary talking and laughing, and will soon pass by like lightning. Where is the effect?

Literacy Education Movement 247

— Er Lang

Reports say that Shanghai will mobilize the entire city to implement compulsory literacy education starting on July 1st. This is something that deserves attention. According to the mayor's report, three-fifths of Shanghai's 3.5 million people live in the urban area, and two-fifths live in the concessions; three-fifths of those living in the urban area, about 2 million people, are estimated to have 500,000 illiterate people (these 500,000 people are from 13 to 50 years old). In other words, among the 2 million people in the urban area, there are 500,000 illiterate adults, and the Education Bureau estimates that there are 150,000 school-age children from 6 to 13 years old who are out of school. The total number of illiterate people is 650,000! This is really an alarming number!

Now, to implement compulsory literacy education, the urban area of ​​Shanghai will be divided into 22 districts, with 10 schools in each district, 6 classes in each school, and each class divided into adult and child classes, with a quota of 50 people. Classes are held three times a day, morning, afternoon, and evening. The first phase will graduate in one month, teaching them to recognize 600 characters in the middle of February, and be able to understand and use them. In addition to setting up schools, a literacy education service team is also organized, with principals, teachers, and staff of primary and secondary schools in the city and older students as the organizational center. All civil servants and party members also join this team. People in the team go to people's homes or go out to find illiterate people to teach them. Then, literacy education mutual aid groups are organized in families, factories, or shops. Literate people in each unit organize a mutual aid group. All illiterate people in the unit who cannot go to school are helped to teach them, so that illiterate people who cannot go to school also have the opportunity to become literate, and those who are not literate at the end of the period will be punished! This kind of plan is very thorough, and it will not be difficult to eradicate illiteracy in Shanghai from now on.

However, the human instinct is to be eager to learn. Just look at how children always ask adults again and again when they encounter things they don't understand, and you can know this. However, may I ask, are the 650,000 illiterate people in Shanghai willing to be aware of the words? They were born to be rejected from the school gates by life for the sake of living. Now that they want to become literate, how can they not be happy, but they have to work all day long to eat, where can they find the time to allow them to become literate? When implementing compulsory literacy education in the future, I think it is best to do this: for illiterate people who do not have a fixed job, give them wages in proportion to their work every day and ask them to concentrate on becoming literate; and for illiterate people in factories and shops, order the factories and shops to allow them to stop work for two hours every day to become literate (wages are not deducted). This is the only way.

The End of Two Months 248

— Hu Weixiong

—Mountain Residence Notes—

Coming here to the mountains was during the winter solstice; although it was the season of falling leaves, it was infinitely exciting to come from a city where there was nothing. Those bald mountain trees, the quiet clear streams, I sent two months of time quickly, and now it is spring!

Holding my younger brother's hand, I stepped out of my friend's house and glanced at this secluded hut for the last time, and I couldn't help but feel hurt. This is a warm and cozy room, a resting place for the withered soul of a wanderer. After a short gathering of two months, now it is a wandering in the north and south again! From my friend's house directly to the small road of the river pier, the mountains and forests around me were blown by the spring breeze, that is, a few unknown migratory birds, now it is goodbye, but when will we meet again? I slowly walked forward, staggering like a camel, wanting to say goodbye to them for the last time, but it seemed that the way ahead was obscured by fog, and I could only hear the beating of my own heart. This is the morning after a new rain has cleared, and there is no sound of footsteps on the mud road that is like velvet.

The seven-year-old younger brother also lowered his head and walked slowly. Was his weak heart also hurt by the separation? If there was no accidental opportunity this time, we would never have known each other. Accidental gatherings and inevitable departures, we cannot be so emotional. That is just a seven-year-old child, it is too cruel to make him hold on to perhaps indelible images! When we came to the stream where our journey was blocked by the small river on a snowy day, I pointed to the green pine and asked him: "Whose tomb is that?" Obviously it was casual.

He raised his head, met my gaze, and a pair of black and large little eyeballs rotated so innocently, "I asked grandma, it is the ancestral tomb of a former high-ranking official." He jumped lively onto the blue stone where we had rested last time, and made a gesture of looking forward.

"Uncle Shanghai, I can't see it. Grandma said there is a very, very big tomb inside."

I also jumped onto that blue stone, and peered through the dense pine forest, but it was just a collapsed earth mound. "The descendants of the former high-ranking official's family are probably declining, right? The weeds on the ancestral tomb are already so tall." Thinking in my heart, I lied to the child:

"Yes, it's very, very big!" I laughed deliberately, "That day we sat here thinking it was the end of the road, but we didn't know there were still many, many beautiful sights ahead."

"My grandma doesn't like me to come out, Uncle Shanghai." He tilted his head and thought, "When I went home that day, I told grandma that we had finished walking the mountain road, and I didn't know if there were any fun places outside. Grandma asked me where I went that day, I said there was a small river in front, and the right hand side was a very large forest - grandma listened and laughed for a long time, and told me that it was the ancestral tomb of a high-ranking official's family, and in the past there was half a mountain this big -.

While talking and talking, I almost forgot to catch the first small steamship. I should be so grateful to my friend for his hospitality during these two months in this scenic spot! Even if you stand here for another ten or eight years, you will have to leave one day. "This is not your home!" That oppression that seemed to kill people, I hugged him down from the green stone and said:

"Let's go, the small steamship has already called out! Next time I come here, I will bring a photo to make it even more interesting."

The child heard that he would bring a photo and clapped his hands and said, "Dad always said he would take me to Shanghai to take pictures. That thing must be fun, taking pictures that look like real people." He thought for a long time, hesitatingly, "Uncle Shanghai, tell Dad to take me to Shanghai, Shanghai is fun!"

I patted his head gently, "I told your dad, I'll come to the mountain to pick you up, okay?"

"Then, come in the summer," he called out as if he had allowed him to go to Shanghai, "Let's go to the back of the mountain to play, there are many, many beautiful flowers, called - grandma said it."

He scratched his head and smiled at me, expressing his apology.

The river pier was already in sight, and the small steamship called out a second time, so I took his hand and hurried forward.

The Wind of Lingnan 249

— Jingfu

This year's spring is still so bleak, and when the cold wind blows over, it falls into the depressed chest, carrying an infinite meaning of tenderness, making people slightly wrinkle the ripples of a stagnant heart. After all, it is the spring wind! I murmured to myself with a bit of amazement.

Such a spring wind, blowing on my heart like this, cannot help but stir up endless sorrow!

It was the scenery of many years ago, I don't remember clearly. However, the spring wind of Lingnan, that taste, is still floating in my confused memory, floating... floating my heart so sour! The spring wind of Lingnan that makes people miss!

An innocent, pure white jade-like child's heart, leaping in the gentle and beautiful spring wind of Lingnan, is always joyful, happy, and there is no trace of the gray walls of the clear and beautiful scenery, people's hearts! However, these things have disappeared like smoke and dreams so silently and completely. The childhood heart, the Lingnan wind of childhood, may never be found again! This is even more unbearable! After the happy year-end of the old year passed, and the spring procession was just over, the spring breeze was warm; the green mountains, the green waters, the gentle and beautiful scenery matched the peaceful and secluded countryside. Children playing and jumping were scattered everywhere, countless happy toys! People worked at sunrise and rested at sunset, and they were so loving and kind. They happily sowed seeds and transplanted seedlings full of hope. Soon the green and vigorous rice fields echoed the gentle shouts of the farmers and their wives. The trees were near the mountains and rivers, secluded and quiet, the streams flowed slowly, the birds chirped softly, the warm wind drifted slowly, and the green water rippled with beautiful and gentle waves; the bamboo forest rustled and played; the hard-working couples stopped to greet them, and the wind blew comfortably; the pedestrians fluttered their clothes and walked leisurely; the children watched the dancing willow leaves and jumped happily. How intoxicating is the gentle wind blowing through all this secluded and beautiful scenery!……

However, remembering these old scenes, I am even more sadly hearing the incessant, wailing from Lingnan... That distant Lingnan, the wind that is floating, is no longer the gentle and light spring wind! But the crying, bloody wind, blowing alone through the desolate and broken wasteland!

Crossing the towering mountains and ridges, like a deep, bottomless wasteland and forest, after drilling through the ten thousand peaks, you can reach the hometown of Lingnan inside the Phoenix Mountain. Gazing at the rustling bamboo forest of Chen's Garden on the side, countless pink and white high houses are listed on the hillside, and the ancient and majestic North Mountain Palace stands out beautifully, and the pine trees in front of the palace are lush and facing the water, as if they are right in front of me! However, now, the North Mountain Palace has been burned, the pine trees have withered, there are few bamboo forests left in Chen's Garden, and the pink and white high houses have become scattered, dilapidated, ruined walls, and mixed with tiles and soil. There is no smoke from the cooking, and no longer can the sounds of chickens and dogs be heard. In the spring fields, there is no green rice, no herders, no jumping children, and no loving and mutual response sounds. The spring wind sweeps across the mountains and rivers that seem to have died, only carrying a strong smell of blood! The wind of Lingnan has completely changed!……

"Who doesn't say that our Phoenix is ​​a paradise, but we have been disturbed by several wars, and then bandits have looted us many times. Farmers can't make a living, and they have to encounter disasters... It's over, it's over, the countryside is scattered and people are dead," the spring wind of Lingnan has become a bloody wind!

Returning Song 250

— Ye Fei

Quietly stepping onto the road back home, I thought like this in my heart, thinking;

The home of a wanderer, you are too far away from me!

One year, two years, three years... I have been wandering like this, wandering; in a foreign land, at the crossroads; I have never missed that distant hometown before, let alone thought about the home I left more than ten years ago.

I have been away from my hometown for exactly eleven years. In these long eleven years, I have only wandered in a few cities; although my mother often writes like this:

"Yun, you have been away from home for more than ten years. You should come back for a visit and see your elderly grandmother; your sisters and brothers also miss you very much..."

Yes! I should have gone back for a visit long ago; to see what the hometown is like after more than ten years, and my grandmother and mother must be older than before, right? My sisters and brothers will also be surprised when they see me, a young man in his twenties, has become so haggard!

My home is in Jiangnan, which is a famous water town. It is surrounded by water, and our home is on a isolated island that stands tall in the raging waves. There is no road to pass through here, and there are only civilian boats on the waterway. Therefore, my unwillingness to go back in the past was also largely related to my fear of taking civilian boats. Now I heard that there are small steamboats running, which has made me, a traveler who has been wandering outside for more than ten years, rekindle the thought of homesickness.

(Go for a visit! After all, the hometown is lovely, and the old home is also worth missing. What's more, there is also my grandmother and mother who miss me; my sisters and brothers are also looking forward to the return of this wanderer!)

No, how should I go back now? Is the wanderer who has been wandering for more than ten years just going back like this? I should bring some success that the elders expect to comfort them! But there is nothing, nothing! Only a body of a man in his twenties that has been worn out by life, and a face that is so old and thin that it looks like a man in his thirties—isn't it too disappointing for them to go back like this? But what can be done!

Speaking of my own son, I also feel ashamed! After struggling in the city for more than ten years, not only did I not achieve anything, but I only ended up with cold treatment and contemptuous looks. I want to cry when I think of these things, but because my tear glands have long been dry, I finally didn't cry:—when a person wants to cry heartily, but can't cry, that is really more difficult than anything.

The wandering life of more than ten years has given me only endless loneliness, emptiness, sadness and pain; only the bitter tears have been my sympathizers and comforters, but my tears have also been shed in these long years, and now I don't even have this only comfort.

"I am uneasy when I whip my horse to return home. I have never stopped thinking about the darkness of the future. I endure the wind and dew and keep going, just because the hair of my old parents is white." The first time I stepped on the ship heading towards my hometown; on the way back, I poked my head out of the window and looked at the shadow of the hometown mountain gradually approaching in front of me. I couldn't help but feel that "the scenery is still the same, but people are no longer the same!" Then I opened a page of diary and silently wrote the above four sentences:

("The home of a wanderer, you are too far away from me!")

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening: "Shanghai Miss"

Modern customs and styles change anew.

Shanghai’s prosperity is most renowned.

The Shanghai Miss has much good fortune.

Cultivated over several lifetimes to learn to be modern.

She is born into a wealthy family, pampered and accustomed,

With servants attending to her every need.

From a young age, she studies at patriotic schools.

Dancing and singing, she excels in everything.

She is gloriously selected as the queen, full of prestige,

Attracting the competition from male students.

She is filled with the new knowledge of the twentieth century.

Deep love exists between men and women.

She speaks fluent English.

She is vividly energetic and pretends to be genuine.

Her foreign attire is very strange.

Her jade-like figure is tall and graceful, with a beauty that could topple a city.

The barber's service is truly authentic.

Her permed hair resembles a repressed tree spirit.

Her cherry-like mouth is painted with a dot of red.

French lipstick is most welcomed.

Her willow-like eyebrows are curved like a new moon.

Her eyes ripple slightly, and her figure is graceful.

She frequently adds three shades of white to her fragrant cheeks.

"Mysto" beauty cream warms her heart.

Her spring bamboo-like fingertips are wholly like jade.

The henna-dyed fingernails are quite the fashion.

Her cerulean powdered neck truly has style.

Pushing up the breasts and exposing the chest is a new fashion.

The qipao is narrow and tight all over the body.

Her fragrant sweat soaks her, like dumplings wrapped in dough.

Short trousers and long stockings.

How could she not fear mosquito and flea bites in the burning sun?

Who can compare to her happiness?

Immoral, licentious, arrogant, and extravagant – too inappropriate.

I hope that she will reduce her expenses and awaken from this dream.
