News 254

The Midnight Music Society at No. 66 Min Village, Mintiniyin Road in this city has been working extremely hard since its renovation, and the number of applicants joining the association has been very enthusiastic in recent days. Xu Ruhui, the person in charge of the association, is committed to compiling "New Eighteen Songs of a Nomad Flute" and plans to publish "Weekly Songs" in the near future. After the "Weekly Songs" are printed, the association will send key members to reside at the wireless radio station to teach the new songs, and they are currently planning this. Wu Qishou, the art director of the association, has been commissioned to be responsible for the design, and it will be printed soon. Pre-orders are welcome.

Shen Bao This City Supplement Film Special

Charlie Chaplin, the Comedian, Makes a Comeback 255

— Huang Yingdai

Investing a Million to Film a New Movie, Love Has Matured, Causing a Sensation Throughout the City

The news of Charlie Chaplin, the comedian, has not appeared on the front pages of newspapers for at least three or four years. In these three or four years, we have only occasionally heard news that he will be filming a new movie, but it was not very certain.

After this, we occasionally received news that Chaplin was going to film a new movie, and people paid special attention. Even more, they wanted to know if the new movie was a silent film or a talkie. However, this news soon faded away. At the same time, some people said that after Chaplin returned to the United States, he would make a movie on his own, but in the end, the new movie did not appear before us. Recently, there has been a rumor about Chaplin's family life, saying that he and Paulette Goddard are deeply in love and will soon be married, and that they will co-star in a movie. However, this movie has not yet started, and we have let this piece of news pass unnoticed.

Because the news about Chaplin is very mysterious and unpredictable, many journalists have recently visited him at his home. As a result, people know that he will start filming a new movie soon. The female lead is, of course, Paulette Goddard. If the general public's judgment is correct, then she must be the future Mrs. Chaplin. Because when a reporter went to visit, Chaplin was not at home, so Goddard received him. In short, anyone can see that although she has not married Chaplin, she is now taking care of some of Chaplin's household affairs. Undoubtedly, she will soon be Mrs. Chaplin.

According to Chaplin himself, they will soon co-star in a new movie, which is titled "The Mass". The filming time will be about five months, but it probably will not be released in Los Angeles before August of this year. We recall that Chaplin's first movie took four and a half years to film! Chaplin's new movie, "The Mass," is intended to be greater in every way than any of his previous movies. He personally intends to invest one million US dollars in this new movie, but we can recall that when he made "City Lights," it cost five million dollars! He naturally believes that this huge investment can be recouped after the new movie is released.

Chaplin's new movie will reportedly not have dialogue but will have sound effects. However, Chaplin himself will not say a single word in the movie. The story depicts a typical worker in a high-pressure American factory. Chaplin is a craftsman who assembles screws and is hired in the factory to specialize in assembling screws on the transmission. As the story unfolds, Chaplin is suspended from his job for committing a fault and is even falsely accused of being a Communist leader and imprisoned. From the above, we can see that Chaplin's new movie: (1) depicts the innocent suffering of a worker, and (2) satirizes modern industry. According to Chaplin, the movie does not contain the slightest political element, and he is very confident that it will be welcomed by South African barbarians, Siamese, British, or people from other countries, but the Soviet Union is not included.

Finally, we will discuss the love story between Chaplin and Miss Goddard. This miss is very similar in appearance to Chaplin's early lover, Ieta Boone Elkins. Although Chaplin himself denies that he will marry Goddard, anyone close to Chaplin believes that they will get married immediately after the new movie is finished. Goddard is often at Chaplin's house, and every weekend she is often with Chaplin's two children, Charles Spencer Jr. and Sydney Earl. These two children are currently receiving military training at a military school during their free time. Here, it is not without clues that Chaplin and Paulette Goddard are deeply in love and will soon be married!

Film Reviews

Review of "After Office Hours" 256

— Hualun

From the perspective of material selection, scriptwriting, and performance, "After Office Hours" is not much different from "The Easiest Way," which was recently starred by the same male lead, Clark Gable. Although its content is empty, the scriptwriting skills are clear, elegant, and exquisite. These are quite suitable for leading actors such as Clark Gable, the so-called screen heartthrobs. This may be the advantage of this type of movie.

Now, let's first talk about the scriptwriting method. Here, the producers and directors simply used more than 20 scenes to perform a fairly wrong plot and exert a not very shallow acting skills. The love between Sharon Norwood, a socialite, and James Brach, an editor of a certain newspaper, is the warp, and the murder case formed by the love triangle between Tommy, Sharon, and rich businessman Mr. Baterson is the woof. The progress is quite in line with the three-act stage play. The introduction is from the newspaper editor's acquaintance with the female reporter and the three photos of the photographer to the separation of the five people with ulterior motives in the Dongjiang Water Nightclub. From Sharon's throwing herself into Tommy's arms to the unfolding of the murder case, this section is the development and also the twists and turns from James and the photographer's re-investigation of Tommy's residence to Sharon's wavering towards Tommy is the climax. If it ended here, the whole play would not feel like it was missing anything. However, the author ended with a happy ending, which is an old cliché.

This kind of drama may be very beautiful. Then, art, including movies, naturally does a considerable job of beautifying life. It's just that it is still a bit regrettable that, in addition to beautification, it also unintentionally exposes a bit of the face of New York society. For example, the ambiguity between the wife of a rich businessman and the legal advisor cannot be resolved. When the advisor falls in love with a beautiful young girl, he does not hesitate to use murder. The fact that the editor of the yellow newspaper, the photographer, and others do not hesitate to risk their lives to obtain such news to increase newspaper sales is also revealed in sweet kisses and passionate love.

Following the exquisite scriptwriting, the director achieved great results: simple, clean, clear, fast, and powerful. It's just that it has not yet gotten rid of many unnecessary things, such as the maid's slapping people, the awkward posture during the boxing fight, etc., which, in addition to low-level fun to make people laugh, have no meaning related to the content. As for the long section of the chase in the wilderness, it is simply redundant. The modification and description of the characters are also not perfect. In the nightclub, when James and Sharon are busy talking about love, a pair of noble guests come to say hello, which increases the psychological expression of the two and also explains Sharon's identity as a socialite, which is still acceptable. The fact that James fought Tommy twice, losing the first three times and winning the last three times, inevitably blurred his personality.

In terms of acting skills, Clark, in addition to his earnestness and considerable activity, does not seem to be better than in his past movies. The female lead, Constance Bennett, is inevitably disappointing. She has almost become a self-less expression, just lengthening the background of others.

Review of "Adorable" 257

— Zhaoren

Xin Guang

Regarding "Adorable," we cannot help but say a few words about the leading actress, Janet Gaynor. Chinese audiences are really too familiar with her, and she made people shed a lot of tears in movies such as "Seventh Heaven," "Angel," and "Street Angel." Therefore, her demeanor has left a deep impression on people. Almost old ladies who don't often watch movies can recognize that it is Janet Gaynor. People are really too familiar with her. Therefore, the opening of "Adorable" at Xin Guang can just illustrate that movie merchants know the audience's psychology well; watching Janet Gaynor is the same as watching Hu Die in "Twin Sisters" or "Rebirth Flower."

In Frank Borzage's "Seventh Heaven" or "Angel," Janet Gaynor is a pure-hearted woman who has won great sympathy for her miserable life as a poor daughter. Similarly, in "Street Angel," she still appeared before the audience in the same posture. However, after "First Year Honeymoon," she broke up with Charles Farrell, who was considered a screen couple, and she also began to appear in a relaxed posture. Of course, this is closely related to the trend of relaxation throughout American movies. Everyone wants to be relaxed and cheerful, and Janet Gaynor is, of course, no exception. She can no longer earn people's tears with sadness, nor can she amuse people with so-called lively sweetness.

However, in recent years, she has gradually become estranged from Chinese audiences. Until now, "Adorable" is only three or four movies. At the same time, she no longer shocks people as she did before. Almost all of them are ordinary and cannot give people a deeper impression. People sigh that Janet Gaynor has fallen from grace.

Now let's look at "Adorable". First of all, the story is fictional, which does not arouse people's interest. Would you believe it? In Central Europe, there is a kingdom that cannot be found on the map. There, a notary suddenly falls in love with a lower-ranking lieutenant and then arbitrarily promotes him. … It is very clear that it is a nonsensical absurdity without any truth. Just like that, the playwright thought that it was not funny enough, not enough drama conflicts, so he brought in a prince from a neighboring country to form a love triangle, making many princes and ministers make many jokes. Under these kinds of jokes, we can only patiently listen to the jokes, but we cannot get any other meaning.

The most brilliant scene is the appearance of the emperor. The playwright and director used exaggerated methods to make the audience guess that the emperor must be a remarkable and powerful figure. However, the final appearance was a seven- or eight-year-old puppet emperor. Therefore, the audience laughed loudly. This climax of laughter, as the end of the play, is not a brilliant scene, but people cannot recognize its deep satirical meaning.

As mentioned above, we cannot but say that director Wilhelm Dieterle's technique is skillful. Whether it is in the mood, the picture, or the sound, he has excellently grasped the relaxed fun. In particular, the dance scenes are quite gorgeous, which adds a golden coat to this empty story. However, we cannot see Janet Gaynor's superb acting skills here. She, like the male lead Henry Garat, is just doing her job plainly. This proves that she is not very suitable for appearing in this kind of light comedy.

Publication of "Movie Stars" Photo Album 258

The "Movie Stars" photo album, which was once widely publicized, is the essence of beautiful photos of the top ten female stars, has been published. The contents include close-ups and private lives of the top ten female stars such as Hu Die, Xu Lai, Chen Yanyan, Yuan Meiyun, Li Lili, Chen Yumei, Ye Qiuxin, Li Zhuozhuo, Li Minghui, and Wang Renmei. There is also an attached story about Ms. Ruan Lingyu's life and death and posthumous glory. All the photos are taken by famous photographers and are unseen in other publications. The beauty of the lens and the refinement of the printing make it outstanding among general Chinese film publications. The price is low, only 20 cents per copy. The publication is edited by Chen Jiazhen, and the liveliness of its layout is self-evident. Movie fans should have a copy. All bookstores sell it. For mail orders, please send 20 cents for postage to He Publishing House, No. 54 Nanjing Road, Shanghai.

Film Novel

The Little Minister (5) 259

— Zhi

The Scots are originally passionate people. They feel that Babbie is more important to Lady Carmichael than she is to herself. She is completely different from the ordinary Gypsy woman. They can't help but admire her in their hearts. Lady Carmichael is already busy coming down to ask what's going on. At the same time, the door opened. A person rushed in, his face pale, and said, "When the minister arrived at the church, many people had not yet dispersed. Peter had locked the door and would not allow it to be opened for the minister to enter. Li Dao held a knife and wanted him to open the door, but Peter finally refused. When he stabbed Peter, the minister shielded him with his body. So he was seriously injured. They are about to carry him here. Has no one gone to call a doctor?" Immediately, more than ten people said, "Go and call a doctor quickly!" Soon, Carmichael was carried back, and his clothes were covered in blood. He stood at the door and said, "Okay, now you're all here. You can convict me of anything." When he saw Babbie, he continued, "I was with her when I should have been at the church tonight. You probably want to say I'm a criminal, but none of you know. She is the one I chose. If you think she is worthless, then I am just as worthless. We are in love. God has blessed me:?" He closed his eyes as he said this, but continued, "...God has blessed me and made her belong to me, and no one can separate us."

He almost fell after he finished speaking. Thomas helped him to bed. Lady Carmichael cried and said, "Poor my son. God won't let you be unhappy." He slowly replied, "Don't cry. Have you seen Babbie?" "Oh, she is so lovely, and we are already good friends." At that time, Babbie leaned down to comfort him, saying that it was all her fault. She comforted him, saying, "Darling, when shall we get married?" He looked at her and smiled, answering, "I hope tomorrow." "Then let's get married when you're better. Then Mr. Thomas and Mr. Spence will be our witnesses, right?" She said, looking at those two elders with her eyes imploringly. Thomas was still hesitating. After Spence pushed him with his hand, they both agreed at the same time.

The doctor came, and everyone left except for a few elders who were still in the room, and Babbie was still with Carmichael. Babbie leaned against the door, looking up and clasping her hands, desperately praying to God. Those elders were all looking at her, and her faith had moved them. After one night, Carmichael was no longer in danger. Then Lord Rildore came to visit Carmichael in person. Of course, Babbie knew as soon as she opened the door that this was his excuse. She told him the whole situation from beginning to end. After he heard it, he said, "Do you love him that much? Don't you have any pity for me?" She replied gently, "Although you are not happy now, you will forget soon. You don't love me at all." "You want good food and good living, everything is luxurious. There is none of that here. Can you endure it? I can buy you anything in the world. Isn't that loving you?" "You don't understand what love is. He cherishes me like this in everything, so I want to cherish him in the same way." Rildore said, "Babbie, I really don't understand you. You have completely changed."

At that time, Lady Carmichael came out and said, "Babbie, he wants to see you." Babbie said goodbye and continued to ask the Duke, "Really, even I don't understand myself. But isn't love created by God? So, if a woman falls in love with someone, God will definitely help her." Lady Carmichael continued, "When we have love, God protects us. Babbie, go in, but don't be too long. He is still weak. He needs your strength. May God bless you." (The End)
